#[global] Unset Universe Checking.

(************************************************************************

 The bicategory of objects with an endomorphisms


 Note: if we would have defined this bicategory via algebras on a
 pseudofunctor, then we would have obtained a different notion of 1-cell.
 In this file, we define it in such a way, that the commutativity cell
 of 1-cells do not have to be invertible.

 Contents
 1. The definition via displayed bicategories
 2. The univalence

 ************************************************************************)

mh: h ¬∑ mz ==> my ¬∑ h

‚Ä¢ ((f ¬∑ g ‚óÉ mh)
   ‚Ä¢ (lassociator (f ¬∑ g) my h
      ‚Ä¢ ((rassociator f g my ‚ñπ h)

            ‚Ä¢ ((lassociator f mx g ‚ñπ h)
               ‚Ä¢ (((mf ‚ñπ g) ‚ñπ h)
                  ‚Ä¢ rassociator (mw ¬∑ f) g h)))))) =

‚Ä¢ (rassociator f g (h ¬∑ mz)
   ‚Ä¢ ((f ‚óÉ (g ‚óÉ mh))

            ‚Ä¢ ((f ‚óÉ rassociator mx g h)
               ‚Ä¢ (lassociator f mx (g ¬∑ h)
                  ‚Ä¢ (mf ‚ñπ g ¬∑ h)))))))

‚àè (a b c d : B) (f : B ‚ü¶ a, b ‚üß) (g : B ‚ü¶ b, c ‚üß)
(h : B ‚ü¶ c, d ‚üß)
(w : disp_end_prebicat_1_id_comp_cells a)
(x : disp_end_prebicat_1_id_comp_cells b)
(y : disp_end_prebicat_1_id_comp_cells c)

(hh : y -->[ h] z),
ff ;; (gg ;; hh)%mor_disp ==>[
lassociator f g h] (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp ;; hh

‚àè (a b c : B) (f1 f2 : B ‚ü¶ a, b ‚üß) (g : B ‚ü¶ b, c ‚üß)
(r : f1 ==> f2)
(x : disp_end_prebicat_1_id_comp_cells a)
(y : disp_end_prebicat_1_id_comp_cells b)
(z : disp_end_prebicat_1_id_comp_cells c)
(ff1 : x -->[ f1] y) (ff2 : x -->[ f2] y)
(gg : y -->[ g] z),
ff1 ==>[ r] ff2 ‚Üí ff1 ;; gg ==>[ r ‚ñπ g] ff2 ;; gg

   ‚Ä¢ lassociator f‚ÇÅ my g) ‚Ä¢ (mf‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ g))

     ‚Ä¢ lassociator f‚ÇÇ my g) ‚Ä¢ (mf‚ÇÇ ‚ñπ g))
   ‚Ä¢ rassociator mx f‚ÇÇ g)

mg: g ¬∑ mz ==> my ¬∑ g

((((f‚ÇÅ ‚óÉ mg) ‚Ä¢ lassociator f‚ÇÅ my g) ‚Ä¢ (mf‚ÇÅ ‚ñπ g))
 ‚Ä¢ rassociator mx f‚ÇÅ g) ‚Ä¢ (mx ‚óÉ (Œ± ‚ñπ g)) =

 ‚Ä¢ (mf‚ÇÇ ‚ñπ g)) ‚Ä¢ rassociator mx f‚ÇÇ g
